1)
The Fulfillment of the Will and Our Responsibility
Here, the Korean residents living in Japan who came yesterday…. According to the report from the leader of the Unification Church in Japan, it becomes clear that Japan will have to take a difficult path in the future in Asia, and that it cannot avoid this. The teacher anticipated this situation in advance and has been making maximum efforts in the United States until this spring on how to connect Japan with China and Korea. 
From a principled perspective, the current situation in Asia and the providential nations of the West
Originally, I thought that if Korea, Japan, and Free China could unite and stand in a position to align with the heavenly direction, they could defend Asia. Geographically, looking at Asia in relation to the West and the East, China is, from our perspective, an archangelic nation. 
Therefore, Korea, Japan, and China are the countries that will be problematic at the end. The area where these three countries are bordering is the last point where the end can be crossed, which can be understood from a principled standpoint. 
When advancing toward a new history in providence, everything must be centered around a sacrificial nation. 
May 18, 1973 (Friday), Belvedere Training Center (New York, USA).
* This speech was given during a leaders' meeting, and the title was added by the editor.
8   The Fulfillment of the Will and Our Responsibility
Therefore, how do we connect Korea, Japan, and China? The nation of Korea cannot exist by itself. Without uniting with Japan, there is no future path. Also, Japan has no way forward without losing China. 
As you know, Free China was expelled from the United Nations General Assembly in October 1971. It has fallen to a position where it has lost its status as an archangelic nation. 
Then, what kind of nation is the United States, which represents the democratic world against the communist bloc? From our perspective, it is the archangelic nation that represents the democratic world and the Western Hemisphere. Therefore, if the United States does not connect with the path of the will in the future, the world will have to pay a great price of many crosses and sacrifices, which is a principled view. 
Until now, what the teacher has emphasized to former Prime Ministers and current key members of the Liberal Democratic Party behind the Japanese government through Kuboki is, “No matter what, do not lose the United States. If you let go of the United States, Japan will lose its archangel and will be blocked in its path.” This has been taught, and such aspects have been instilled. If Japan and the United States were to break off, it would be problematic. 
Looking at Japan itself, Japan has already severed all diplomatic ties with Free China. 
Now, there are many difficult issues regarding getting Japan and the United States to join hands in the future. Who will do that? It is entering a stage that is difficult for those countries themselves to handle. Therefore, it remains a problem that we must address. 
Now, we must engage in new binding activities in the United States, which is why the teacher began to develop operations focused on 1972. Here, we must quickly create a standard where the three countries (Korea, Japan, and the United States) can unite internally. 
Such operations will be expanded to Europe next. 
We are connecting Europe to this. Why connect Europe to this? Because, centered around the West, if the United States is an Adam-type nation, then England is a sun-type nation. 
Then, what nation would be the ultimate archangelic nation? It is Germany that is regarded as the global archangelic nation at the end. It must be a nation that is not in a divided position. 
From this perspective, the United States is an Adam-type nation representing the Western civilization sphere. When looking at Asia and the West, if Asia is Abel, then the West is Cain, so the United States must be that representative nation. 
Therefore, if there is a failure in Asia, what will happen? It can shift to the Western civilization sphere. If the final battle is to be decided centered on the United States, England, and Germany, then the failures in Asia can be rectified here. Therefore, the operations that the teacher has been conducting since last year are aimed at transferring the internal foundation laid in Asia directly to the Western world. Holding revival meetings and connecting in this way. 
Everyone, we must exert total effort until next year, 1974. This applies to both Japan and Korea, and we are at a stage where the internal situation and external circumstances must align for the final decision to be made. 
In Japan, until the second seven-year course, or in Korea, until the second seven-year course, the question is how to connect this internally and externally with all sincerity. Until the second seven-year course ends, how to center around the second seven-year course…. The second seven-year course is at the growth stage, so if the first seven-year course was the path taken centered on the parents, the second seven-year course is similar to the children’s seven-year course. Therefore, the second seven-year course is a period in which the children must inherit the path taken by the parents and fight the same battles that the parents fought in Japan, Korea, or China. 
When Kuboki came the other day, what I said was…. We must take responsibility for Japan, but Japan, which should have protected China and Korea until now, has taken such a position that it has failed to fulfill its responsibility to defend Korea and distance itself from China, so I specifically instructed that you must take responsibility for Korea and China for two years. 
10   The Fulfillment of the Will and Our Responsibility
Since 1974 is a time when a seven-year course is transitioning, if a standard is not established by then, important officials in both Korea and Japan will all have to move to the United States. The current situation in Korea is urgent. It is reaching its peak. Japan is the same. Free China is also in a similar situation. 
The Internal Power Struggle Targeting Japan and the Final Base, England
Everyone, currently, China and the Soviet Union are in a state of internal conflict and disconnection. Looking at it centered on Free China, Japan does not support Free China. Since Japan has stated that Free China is part of China, it has automatically led China to consider Taiwan as its territory. In other words, since Japan has recognized Free China as part of China, China now considers Free China as its territory. 
Thus, Free China, which could only trust Japan, cannot rely on Japan to support Free China, and now has no choice but to align with the Soviet Union. The Soviet Union has been planning to move its military bases in the border areas with China southward, making the Indian Ocean a base they can operate from, and is now preparing to completely blockade China’s maritime rights from Taiwan through Vladivostok centered on Singapore. The Soviet Union has realized that it is quite difficult to confront China on land due to population issues and various other problems, but ultimately, through maritime rights, China is in a defenseless state, and they have been able to position themselves to gain superiority based on this. 
However, why has the Soviet Union not touched maritime rights until now? Because the United States' Seventh Fleet has been defending and protecting the Taiwan Strait, they have not been able to intervene. However, now the United States is in a position where it cannot take responsibility for Taiwan. Also, regarding Asia and Vietnam, it is in a position where it cannot take responsibility…. As this happens, the original purpose of sending the Seventh Fleet to defend Asia seems to have completely collapsed, and now the Seventh Fleet of the United States is in a position where it must retreat. 
Now, as Taiwan aligns with the Soviet Union, naturally, Soviet troops will enter the Taiwan Strait. However, can the U.S. Seventh Fleet confront the Soviet fleet? Currently, it cannot confront them, so the Soviet Union is aware of this and is strongly pushing forward. The other day, I saw in the news that there is an island called Penghu, located between the Chinese mainland and Taiwan, where there are articles suggesting that a Soviet naval base should be established…. If that happens, from Vladivostok through the Taiwan Strait and Singapore, the entire maritime area of the Indian Ocean can become a base for the Soviet fleet. 
Why is that? What the Soviet Union desires is to defend China while simultaneously bringing Japan under its control. It aims to defend against Chinese invasion. In doing so, it intends to apply pressure on China while approaching Japan with these two objectives. 
Now, looking at Japan, both China and the Soviet Union are trying to bring Japan under their control, and you should know that the Japanese Communist Party is affiliated with the Soviet camp. Therefore, both China and the Soviet Union are throwing their utmost interest and overtures toward the Japanese government. The question is how to block this, and the way the Soviet Union can take the initiative is to block the communication between China and Japan. If they block maritime rights, it is considered blocked. In this way, the Soviet Union will enter a position of superiority. 
You may not know, but recently, Soviet planes have been patrolling Japan from Sakhalin once a day on average. Currently, more than 230,000 Soviet troops are deployed in Sakhalin. That is north of Japan. Looking at Japan in this situation, as you know, it has entered a stage where the Socialist Party and the Communist Party can gain power, and all the mayors of the 137 major cities are members of the Communist Party. 
12   The Fulfillment of the Will and Our Responsibility
Now, nearly three hundred members of various economic delegations from China are in Japan, and we can see that they are engaging in internal power struggles with the Soviet Union over Japan. Ultimately, the Soviet Union and China are engaged in internal power struggles to expand their bases concerning Japan. 
Currently, it appears that Japan is moving into the sphere of influence of the Soviet Union. If Japan were to return to being a Communist Party under the Soviet Union, the entire country would become a Soviet naval base and a base for the Soviet Union concerning Asia. Then, it would become a direct confrontation with the United States over the Pacific. 
Therefore, no matter how much Nixon dislikes it, after 1976, he will inevitably have to return to take responsibility for Asia, according to the teacher's view. No matter how much he retreats, he will have to return again. In returning, he will be faced with great enemies, with hundreds of times the enemies, and must be prepared to make life-and-death decisions. Then, does the United States have the power to handle that? The teacher believes it does not. 
So who should take responsibility for that? We must prepare for that from now on. Everyone, look at Europe. The teacher has also mentioned this in Europe, but France, Germany, and currently Italy are all being swept into the Communist sphere, so our final base in Europe will be England. Therefore, I instructed everyone to prepare to go to England in case of urgency. Currently, the attempt to do stainless steel painting in England is also an economic preparation for such issues. The people of Europe are not prepared at all. 
The Last Path to Block Communism Worldwide and Joining the WCC
Now, looking at the world, a time is coming soon when we must make a judgment about our fate. Who will take responsibility for that? Only we can. That is why the teacher has been most concerned about the fact that the Christians in the United States have no interest in the country. Christians cannot protect the country, and after meeting with senators, I found that none of the senators are willing to protect the country. They are worried about their own elections but do not care about the country collapsing. They have such a mindset and way of thinking. 
So what should we do about this? What kind of movement should we undertake in the United States? We must engage in a movement to reunite Christians. To do this, we have separated politics and religion until now, but we must combine them so that religious people can move politics. Before that movement, I believe there is no way to involve Christians. 
Ultimately, when we look at senators and such people, they cannot do without the color of religion. People who believe in God must protect this country. Senators should also stand at the forefront and become those who advocate God's will, standing in a position to move the whole. However, they have all become opportunists. 
The purpose of this movement is not just to protect America but to block communism. It is to block communism. By conducting such a movement in the United States, the global Christian community must create a worldwide Christian party that can politically move the governments of each country to defend the world from the clutches of communism. That is what the teacher believes we must do.
When there is a threat from the Communist Party, Christianity must mobilize the youth across borders to defend that country before there is a way to stop the threat of the communist world. Truly, if Christians from all over the world do not unite to provide unlimited support in terms of economic and human resources to places invaded by communism, we must do so. The teacher sees this as the last resort to stop communism worldwide.

Despite America being the representative nation of Christian democracy, can America stop communism? It cannot. Therefore, we have no choice but to focus on Christian ideals and carry out a revival movement to strengthen global organizations and foundations. The first thing we must do as a leading effort is to quickly join the World Council of Churches (WCC). Once we join, we will have many young elites and be engaged in a global movement, so it will definitely become an issue within three years. We must raise the issue.

In a world where Christianity is facing the urgent threat of communism externally and is internally divided, if we provide our principles, it will become a good opportunity to hold onto. Then, this will quickly emerge as a global issue. We must suppress the top rather than fighting Christianity individually. Currently, Christianity is having a revival movement centered around Billy Graham. We must do more than that. We need to create a foundation to present issues beyond that. The teacher's plan is to begin negotiations with them from now on. If that does not happen, we will have to create an organizational foundation to cut off their heads.

Who must do this? You must do it. Therefore, I spoke to Mr. Park and Chairman Kim recently, but the most urgent issue right now is to quickly join the WCC. We are currently investigating this. We are mobilizing task forces and women’s groups to push for negotiations. Without this…

If we do not lay the groundwork to raise issues within American Christianity soon, who will support us? We are running out of time. Therefore, we must lay the groundwork and prepare our offensive posture by 1974; otherwise, there will be no way to stop the impending fate of the world. I found out that to join the WCC, we need at least 25,000 members in the U.S. Only with 25,000 members can we join the WCC in the U.S. If we join here, we will automatically be part of it.

Before the urgent time comes to America, let’s just lay the groundwork. Looking at this global issue, considering the position of the democratic world facing the threat of the communist world, it is becoming an urgent situation in Asia where America must not retreat. And looking at the future Pacific, in about three years, the Soviet Union will be dominant in every aspect. Who will stop this approaching threat? Who will stop it? The Soviet Union is completely ideologically armed, and when they say "let's go," over 200 million citizens can move to one place. But what about America? If these people come and go, everything will fall apart. Do you think there is no underground organization of the Communist Party in America? Also, regarding the black and white issue... in the future, a powerful assassination squad centered on black people will appear in broad daylight. So, all the important people... they will do such things in broad daylight. By the time we say, "Oh no," we will already be in a chokehold, and it will be too late.

In Asia, Korea, Japan, and Free China have ended up like this because they did not listen to the teacher, and now if America does not listen, it will end up like that too. I have been talking about the situation in Japan for 5 to 7 years, and it is all coming true. Our International Victory Federation has taken the lead against the Communist Party in Asia, Japan, and Free China because we have a global organization. But if we are communized, do you think all the Unification Church members will remain? There will be nothing left. Nothing at all.

In this situation, do we have a chance to win or not? Do you have confidence or not? "We do." We must recognize that the Communist Party occupies one-third of the world. How many Unification Church members are there currently? The last statistics showed about 850. Are we going to stop the Communist Party with that? What will we do? We must understand that there is a divine adventure to hasten our path to extraordinary success in driving them out. It is God who opens up an adventurous path that can bring us victory. We must become leaders who can embrace that adventure. You must become courageous enough to take risks. There is no other way. In this desperate time... you cannot think normally and just go out like this. It will not work. It will lead to ruin. Ultimately, there is no other conclusion than to confront with adventurous faith and hold onto God.

We must lay that groundwork not in decades but within just a few years. To do that, we need more people. The teacher's heart and God's heart want to mobilize everyone, including men, women, and even babies in the womb. Even the babies in the womb... In this time, if we give it our all and even if we fail, if we can say, "We did our best," then a way to live will emerge. If we fail without giving our all, there will be no way to live, but if we give our all and fail, resurrection will occur. A way to live will emerge. We are in such a time. Now is that time.

So, is it forward or backward? "Forward." That is not easy. Therefore, in your thoughts, you must not forget the idea that there will be no rest until this war is over, and the idea of being heaven's messenger standing at the forefront to save humanity. Now America is also coming to a desperate time. Before that time comes, let’s just lay the groundwork and plant the flag. Then, if we can say, "If we become like those Americans, we can surely stop and defeat the Communist Party," then the time will come when they will come with red eyes and cannot help but put us in front.

In that sense, the existence of the Communist Party allows us to find the secret to rising quickly. If there were no Communist Party, the Park regime would not need us. The Korean people do not need our ideals. The Japanese people do not need our ideals either. The same goes for China and America. America will surely become like that. All of Europe will also become like that.

There are two issues here. First, the issue of winning through fighting, and the second is how to manage things after winning. These two issues exist. Do you have a plan for that? You must be responsible for that as well. It is not just about winning through fighting. Managing things after fighting is even more problematic.

So, is there such a person? There are no such people, so from now on, after eating, we must educate, and after eating, we must train. What is the method? How should we do it? The American people, the entire democratic world must know that "these people will fight on our behalf." That is one way. How do we instill that ideology into all humanity in the rear? If we can instill that, managing things will not be a problem. Wouldn't it?

Therefore, it is a problem how you enter the nation, unite with all the people, share emotional experiences, cry together, and show everyone that you have taken on the burdens. If we cannot lay this groundwork and do not win, we may be threatened with all heads being cut off in a Communist manner, but that will not work. "Because this happened, you won. Therefore, you all must become our leaders and guide us." We must unite like this, not "What? You fought and won against us?" That cannot happen. You must think about that. No matter how much you think, there is no other way.

Thus, our fighting is ultimately to prepare a way to manage the people in the future, to train to fight and win against the Communist Party. We must realize that we are currently doing these two things. Therefore, we are looking at both aspects of winning and managing. That is why the teacher said not to promote first. We must show and then promote. Therefore, from the state level to the county and village levels, how do we organize this to establish the idea that "only these people can save America or the world"? If we establish that idea, then managing things will be a problem, but the problem until that idea is established is even greater.

Looking at Korea, there are professors and prominent figures saying, "We only believe in the Unification Church. You are the only ones who can save this country, so please bear with us for a few more years." Japan is the same. They say, "Within 15 years, you will be able to move this country, so please fight well." The fact that this has become possible is a result of having faced such environmental conditions and fought. However, that does not mean we have immediate benefits, but the established foundation and our current position are significant benchmarks that have been clearly revealed through our fighting experience.

Let’s risk our lives to evangelize. We must show that we have fought for the world, to save this country, and to love these people, and when we appeal with tears, the masses will say, "That’s right," and we have laid the groundwork for them to cry with us. This is what is terrifying. So, should we do that or not? "We must." There is no other way.

So, you... if you are the task force leader and you get into the van, do you say, "Hey, this car! Hurry up! Hurry up!" Do the task force leaders do that? When young people go to the activity site and unload the luggage, do they say, "What are you unpacking! Leave it there, let’s go!"? Did you go there to unpack the luggage? You went there to meet people and greet them, right? You went there to receive something? No. You went there to give... I’m not going there to eat something delicious. No. You must sincerely give and then come back to receive. If you go to get something delicious, you are a beggar. You are in debt.

Is that principle correct? You must give first. If I am busy and as soon as I arrive, I say, "Let’s hurry up! Let’s hurry up!" If I am that busy, a conscientious person will feel something inside and want to go out and look for something, wanting to meet our people naturally. That is how history works.

Therefore, even if the first day is not possible, the leader must lead. The task force leader must go out with a microphone... Is everyone doing that? And state leaders were told to evangelize one person a month, and if they could not evangelize, they should not eat at all. They should fast for 40 days or be prepared to die, to see if they can evangelize. It will be done.

Now, look. There are currently 850 members, but we need 8,000 by the year after next. Will this be enough? It would be nice if we could say, "It doesn’t have to be that way," but it is not set up like that. We must match this. If we do not match it, we cannot proceed.

So, if we need 8,000 members, what fraction of the country is that? One in 30,000, right? One in 30,000... Can one person move 30,000 people? At that time, we must urgently grab a top senator, grab a governor, and grab the police chief. That is the only way. There is no other way. To do that, we need training to confront those people. Even if we do not have the skills, we must mobilize all our experiences, fighting results, and knowledge to confidently persuade those people. Shouldn’t we do that? Is this country that small? If so... if you all eat whatever you want and do whatever you want, it would be easy... Why does the teacher want to do such difficult things? I am also dying. I am also struggling.

You know, losers do not get sympathy. Therefore, we must win. We must win justly. We must win justly. You must understand that winning justly is many times harder than winning by any means necessary. Would the teacher not be comfortable? How about it? Not in this small Korea, but in this big country... Looking at the world situation, if we do not do it like this, there is no way to stop it. Nevertheless, the teacher does not get discouraged. The teacher has walked the peaks and boundaries of good and evil, so that is how he always lives.

No one has pulled me along saying, "Let’s do it this way." I have pulled everything along. It is not easy to lead these tall people who do not even speak the same language as Korea or Japan. I have to do this with my hands and this with my eyes, but my hands are doing this and my eyes are doing that, and my legs are doing this. (Expressing with gestures) So when I pull, it is a big deal. Inside you, don’t you feel like, "Oh, I’m dying"? Don’t you feel that way inside? You are not the only ones. The missionaries who come here are all saying, "Oh, I’m dying! Oh, I’m dying!" Can we be comfortable like that? What will happen to America? Tell me if there is a way. It is the teacher who talks about methods, who else? Ultimately, there is no other way than the teacher's way. No matter how much you think about it, there is no other way. If you fall away... if you run fast, side effects will occur. Some will fall off, and some will collapse. That is not natural.

Think about it. In a war, is there such a thing as winning without casualties, without death? You must understand that famous wars and famous victories come with proportional sacrifices. There are always sacrifices with famous victories. Do you understand? "Yes."

Is it forward or backward? "Forward." The teacher is here in America...
I hope you will only pull your noses in here, but do I have to take care of the whole world, not just poor Korea? "We have to take care of other countries." Why? If you fail, you need to create a place to escape to. "I will do all this and then go help other countries." From now on, we need to fight and see the results. So, should we tighten our belts or not? "We should tighten them." 

That's why in your mobilization team... I received a report about the mobilization team recently, and if I had seen that they were just slacking off, I would have given all of them a good scolding. You cannot go without converting at least one person a month. Look, to go from 800 to 8,000, you need to risk your life and do it based on one person a month. Still, how many have there been in a year? About 850, so it increased by around 450, about 480, close to 500. Since the beginning of January, in six months. So it has increased. This increase happened because the teacher was strict and made it difficult; if I had left you alone, would it have increased like this?

If things don't go as you wish, be prepared to put in ten times more effort.
Now, based on this standard, we need to push ten times harder than we have until now. If we push ten times harder, 500 will become 5,000. Isn't that right? 

Therefore, based on scientific analysis, we need the mobilization team to work ten times harder, and the regular teams need to operate ten times more. If the body doesn't have time, we need to put in ten times more sincerity. If you slept under a blanket, you should throw the blanket away and sit up to sleep. If not sitting, then you should lie down to sleep. After all, you can sleep well even lying down here, right? (Laughter) You should sleep standing up. Can you do that? "Yes." Do you want to do it happily? "Yes." Then try it, let me watch. Wherever I go, I open my mouth and say, 'Ah, this is good, this is good.' When you meet the teacher, the teacher always has a serious face when dealing with you. So, please make the teacher smile, make him laugh. The teacher is originally cheerful, likes to laugh, and enjoys playing. But he is serious.

Keep that in mind... Now, look, it's a big deal. The United States itself is in big trouble. Where will God go? There is no one to believe in but us, only us. If things don't go as planned, you must be prepared to die. If this mission fails, everyone must be prepared to die on the Pacific coast. What does that mean? It means you must be ready to die while fighting against communism. It has to be that way. There is no other way. If you didn't defend against communism domestically before that fight, then it is acceptable to fail. It means it's acceptable to die. If that happens, you must go out and shoot your sons and daughters with a gun. You must not let them die from a stab by communists. It shouldn't come to that, but you must be prepared for such a resolve.

The only way is to do as the teacher says. There are no other weapons. If you take responsibility and do it instead of the teacher, I will gladly say, 'Go ahead and do it.' The teacher is not someone who likes power or honor. It is only for the purpose, only for humanity... That's all there is.

Now, our conclusion is to move forward. Whether alive or dead, whether sleeping or eating, whether resting or not, we must always move forward. Thinking is moving forward.

Now, after June, the teacher is planning to go to Korea once, and although I couldn't do it for the past five months, how about trying to convert one person each for just this month? "Yes." The mobilization team leader must have that mindset, and the members of the mobilization team as well... Even while eating, the education is all about that. One person a month. Now, I plan to commend the mobilization team leader every six months, and I plan to commend the representative every six months. After that, I will commend those among the mobilization team members and the members of the province who have the most achievements. Every six months, twice a year... I am preparing for that. Well, the responsible people may not be able to take them, but I plan to select the top five or ten among the best-performing members and send them to New York or somewhere to truly engage in decisive battles and activities to achieve results. So, among the ten people, I will select the real one and send them back to their province to establish such a tradition. The provincial leaders will also do the same. The provincial leaders... (followed by a report on activities)

The responsible person must create a team centered around the heart.
Now, raise your hand if you have more than 20 mobilization team members. How many have more than 20 mobilization team members among the team leaders? How many are there? (Responses: 23, 21, 23, 22, etc.) I told you to convert three people and remove one from among them; what happened? When you go around twice, if you convert two people, you remove one. That is the principle we operate on. The older members should be sent out to work, and the converted members should receive education to nurture successors. The mobilization team must plan and organize teams where one person is responsible for education, one for business, and one for evangelism. Even 20 is too few.

You need to think about this. It’s all good that you are giving lectures and holding revival meetings, but revivals should not be done carelessly. You need to give lectures, lectures. How do you master the principles in six months? That is the issue. And evangelize. And solve economic issues. In the future, we need to establish a regular system where if there are three outstanding people, we can keep removing them. They will probably want to hold on tightly and not let go. In other words, the overall mobilization team leader has many excellent people who have been guided in universities, but they will not want to let them go. Ultimately, we do not know how much those who have been educated and sent out will evangelize if they hold onto them.

Therefore, you must nurture people within six months... If the number of people increases, we must change. Everyone must change, but what you must always keep in mind is that the leader who has become responsible should not just bring them in first. One person, one person for three days, one week... If you do it for a week, in six months, how many weeks will that be? Four times six is twenty-four (4×6=24), 24 weeks. So, you should raise one person each week. Do you understand? get out of the way and address it. The issue of whether God exists or not is something that Mr. Choi spoke well about, and we must condense all of this into a clear and concise explanation.

The two main elements that are problematic in philosophy are the idea and matter. The first issue that arises is the "idea." This is where most problems begin. The next issue is matter, which refers to relative material, the material that serves as the relative condition for the idea. These two elements, the idea and matter, constitute the fundamental problems in philosophy. Modern philosophy, as well as ancient philosophy, deals with how to address this issue.
In actual life—when we talk about actual life, we refer to both physical life and mental life—the differences in how we adapt to it give rise to various philosophical forms. 

Therefore, when we look at philosophy, we find that a logic is needed to study the question of how existence exists, and if existence exists, how it is. This leads to the development of epistemology, which examines how we acknowledge that logic. 

From that recognition, issues of actual life arise. When you say, "It is good," or "It is truth, beauty, love," what does that mean? It comes from a concept. It comes from an ideology. Then, where does such an ideology come from? There must be some kind of standard that can possess that ideology.

**Unification Philosophy and Standards**

Thus, truth, beauty, and love themselves cannot be equal to the concept itself. In other words, truth is equal to the concept, but the concept cannot be equal to God. Truth, beauty, and love are abstract nouns that cannot exist alone or be manifested alone. 

Truth cannot be established by itself. Beauty cannot be established by itself. Love cannot be established by itself. So what are truth, beauty, and love? They are merely content expressions that can connect in the middle. 

When we pursue truth, beauty, and love, we enter into a certain concept. However, that concept cannot be vague. It must be concrete. The issue arises that the concrete itself must have some kind of standard. Even if I speak of truth and say I am beautiful, that is truth and beauty, but it is not me. Therefore, there must be a standard that possesses some content, and that standard is what? If it is a person, it must be a person; the 'I' must be defined. If it is God, it must have God's standard, and truth is needed with God's standard, beauty is needed with God's standard, and love is needed with God's standard. Without God's standard, all things related to beauty and love are unnecessary.

Thus, the most problematic aspect of our Unification Philosophy is the concept of 'standards' that has not existed in the philosophical world until now. A man has a standard as a man, and a woman has a standard as a woman. A man is not equal to a woman. Then how do those standards become one? I believe they become one through conditions such as beauty, truth, and love. What is needed to unify those standards is truth, beauty, and love. What does that mean? It means that the conceptual content that can connect the true subject and the true object must be truth, beauty, and love. This must be organized. Without the concept of one, what is truth?

When I see something and say, "Oh, this is really good," it is already happening under the concept of oneness, under the concept of one. When I say, "It is good," it is said under some concept that it has been done according to my will. The issue of how much it connects in front of the standard of oneness is where the question of truth, beauty, and love arises.

**Concepts as Connective Materials for Unification**

Therefore, how do we achieve oneness? We must always organize the concepts of subject and object. Who is the ultimate subject? That is what we call God. When we look at these issues, why is it called Unification Thought? All thoughts are ideas. All ideologies are ideas. It means logical ideas. 

Thought is not me. Beauty is also an abstract noun of relational content, not me. Love is not me either. They are all materials for connecting to create one. They are the materials that facilitate connection. When you say, "I hope to sing well," it is also to create a subject that can be good and an object that can be good. This is the issue that the teacher has pondered upon in philosophical matters.

Thus, the concept of standards must emerge. Without standards, one cannot envision a unified world, a true unified world. Therefore, in the new Unification Thought, the concept of standards will become a major issue in the future of philosophical thought.

**Essence and Interaction**

Now, let’s deduce. When we say, "There is matter," what is matter composed of? It is composed of force. Then what is that force, or energy? It cannot be vague. There must be truth, beauty, love, and goodness in it. Then, does everything get resolved with those things alone? Everything cannot be resolved without the relationship between subject and object. 

Is this relative relationship established only in our relationship with God? If that is the case, it becomes one-sided. Therefore, to prevent that one-sidedness, there must be a horizontal relationship between subject and object. God must also have a subject and object. All humans are also structured that way. That is the concept that emerges.

Thus, in our principles, the term 'essence and form' is a fundamental issue that cannot be overlooked. Do you understand what that means? If two become one, they can go this way, but they cannot go horizontally. Therefore, even God must stop this incoming force and, in order to move in another direction, there must also be a horizontal relationship between subject and object. Here, the term 'God's essence and form' becomes inevitably necessary.

Thus, within God, there must be essence and form. There must be a unified essence and form, and there must be truth, beauty, and love in it. Because of such standards, God needs humans relatively, and humans must be able to receive the inner manifestation. Therefore, in order for humans to become one, they must follow truth, beauty, and love. This is theoretical. Thus, the interaction is established here. Do you understand? The issues of essence and interaction are established here in the principles.

Then, what is interaction for? It is for the purpose of becoming one. How do we become one? It requires going through a step-by-step process, leading to the three stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection. Will becoming one be vague? It cannot just be that God likes it and I like it; the whole must like it. Here, we find the individual purpose, family purpose, and world purpose. It does not end with me and God becoming one; this becomes a motivation for what else can become one, that is, for the development and increase of purpose. This is inevitable. This is the essence of it.

**Truth, Beauty, and Love Established to Create Oneness between Subject and Object**

Therefore, truth, love, and beauty are the contents of concepts, not the subjectivity of concepts. The concept itself cannot be based solely on thought. There must be a standard. The concept of personality must be brought forth. Then what is the standard itself? It must have a standard that can encompass the concepts of all things, and that is God. This is how we see it. "God exists like this. Therefore, God thinks. What does God think? God thinks true thoughts. God thinks beautiful thoughts. God thinks good things. God thinks of love." This must be theoretical. God thinks because God exists, right? Therefore, there must be a standard before the concept. That is what we call God.

Then what are these truths, beauties, and loves for? They are for becoming one with the relative. They are for becoming one. When we become one, the purpose is fulfilled. Then why do we want to fulfill the purpose? Because it will be eternal. To be eternal, we must be one. We must achieve unification. Do you understand that?

Therefore, in order to create oneness between subject and object, philosophy and all the adjectival expressions of beauty that we are currently using must be established. Thus, without subject and object, there is nothing. (While writing) When this becomes one... There is only one way to become one. If it is done through thought, then this way is wrong. There are countless paths in thinking. There are many similar paths. There are many similar thoughts. If this is the case, it is similar, but... it is just similar. Here, one can think in reverse as well.

Complete unification cannot happen the farther away it gets. There is only one path. In the content that can connect this path, the nouns of truth, beauty, and love are established. If you step outside of this, it will go awry. Everyone, truth, love, and beauty are merely process-oriented stimuli that can lead to oneness.

Because of that, greater things... Because of that, the stimulus generates momentum. Without it, it cannot be. That stimulus does not only reach there; it seeks greater stimuli. It seeks greater love, greater beauty, and ultimately reaches a position that can relate to God's dignity. To do that, all of this has been bestowed upon us. (While writing) Here, beauty is established. Then comes love, right? That is here. This must be established. Can you find beauty without subject and object? Can there be love without subject and object? Can you know truth without subject and object?

**Viewing the Universe's Foundation through the Concept of Subject and Object**

Now, therefore, when we enter the origin of existence in the world of existence and seek whether God exists or not, we must first have a concept and then move beyond that to the relationship between subject and object. Everyone, where does all the power in this world come from? That is the question. In other words, force is the cause of matter, but where does it come from? Does force come alone? It does not come alone. Before force can emerge, there must be action. Only then does force come forth. 

Can action happen alone? If I were to do this alone without you, I would be considered insane. All actions and such must occur within the relationship between subject and object. No matter how much force there is, if there is no subject and object, force cannot emerge. Before force can emerge, what must exist? There must be action, and before action, there must be subject and object. This is decisively determined by this concept.

Therefore, the foundation of the universe is the concept of subject and object, rather than force. The cosmic foundation begins with the concept of subject and object, and within that subject and object, there must be standards. There must be subjective standards and relative standards. The subjective standard is God, and the relative standard is humanity. Why did God create humans? Because God is a subject, and without a counterpart, it cannot be. Let's take a look at the environment
Today, let's talk briefly about "Let's take a look at the environment." It could also be said as "Let's pay attention to the environment."

In the changing environment, the digestive and absorptive power of humans
Here, there are both women and men. We know that the life paths of women and men are different. What women think and feel is also different from what men think and feel. Even when looking at the lives of men and women, the stages of youth, young adulthood, middle age, and old age are all different.

Just as it is with our lives, we see that the natural world also changes according to the four seasons. If I have become accustomed to living in summer, I cannot just think about summer and only prepare for summer clothes without considering winter. Likewise, those who lived in winter should not only think about winter. If a person who dressed for winter says, "I hate summer. Why isn't winter coming?" that won't work. What that means is that if you don't prepare your clothes according to the changes, you cannot go through the process of change.

May 25, 1973 (Friday), Belvedere Training Center.
Our life paths are not all the same. Sometimes... those who like summer may think, "Ah, I like this. I like my youth." But that's not all there is. Ultimately, in living a life, we must bring about developmental changes according to environmental changes.

Then, when looking at oneself, is there ever a time when one can say, "I don't like it"? No, there must be. Development must exist. So, does one develop only with good things? No, that's not the case. You see, even in a single day, moods go up and down. If the good moments in a day are just a little more than the bad, that day is considered good. If there are just a little less good moments, that day is considered a retreat. It means that it is not progress but a retreat. The thought that one wishes for an environment without challenges is a common human thought, but it doesn't work that way.

Therefore, while going through these processes of change, how do we digest and absorb them with self-control, and does what is absorbed become a plus or a minus for oneself? We are compelled to walk forward, whether we like it or not, and we are bound to face such environments.

In youth, training is needed to develop the ability to absorb and digest the environment. Generally, the lives of young people are tumultuous. In youth, they like stimulating and ever-changing things. It's fine to like those things, but one must have the ability to absorb and digest the changing environment. If one only likes those things without that ability, they will end up living a life unrelated to themselves. The youth period is a time full of adventure and risk, so a path of learning to discern those things is necessary.

The path of learning, the path that ancestors walked, and the experiences accumulated by all people are essential. And if you do not know the future you will face, this period of youth is indispensable for training to cultivate intrinsic character. Therefore, even in this youth period, no matter how tumultuous life may be, no matter how many challenges arise, we must recognize that training to adjust and overcome all of that is absolutely necessary.

Those who say they need training that suits their hearts but reject training they dislike will become people who cannot achieve a developing character. Then, what attitude should one have? One must take an interest in the events and problems that come their way. When receiving training, one must pay attention to all the processes of training that come their way. Regarding those issues, one should not just look at them but be someone who is interested and measures the situation from all angles. With interest, one should observe how...

Like a whirlpool... for example, there is the Hudson River, but the water that comes through the mountainous areas must have gone through all sorts of courses. It flows through waterfalls, twists, collides with rocks, and goes through various curves. Here, it forms a large river, so it looks nice, but underneath, it flows with countless currents. You often see scenes like that in movies, but when a small boat goes and falls under a twisting waterfall, you cannot just look at that. You must adjust by looking at the front and back; otherwise, there is no way to survive.

Similarly, in your life journey, there will be waterfalls, times when you must face rocks head-on, or times when something will push you to collide without you even hitting it. You must navigate through all these environments. If you say, "I won't go," no matter how much you try not to go, your destined path remains. Just like if water flows into the Hudson River, it is bound to follow the riverbank, whether it likes it or not.

So, is it bad to fall over a waterfall? Or is it bad to go through a winding path, colliding with rocks? No, that's not the case. If one can digest those experiences, they will gain the ability to face even greater challenges afterward. Those who find interest in that, who have the pioneering spirit to face death, and who can digest those processes with joy will find that the path to the great ocean connects more and more.

However, if one does not stand in such a position and says, "Oh, I just dislike it. I won't move at first. I don't like it," can that work? No, it cannot. Such people are like water that cannot meet the great ocean.

7) Protect the path of destiny  
We think that a good place is where we meet good people or have good experiences, but it cannot always be good. It can also be miserable.  
The one who protects with the power of love is the best protector.  
From the world's perspective, let's say someone studies and works hard to take an exam, like a national exam. The moment they take the exam and the results are announced is not necessarily a good moment. They do not know how their destiny will be determined. Even in the highest hope of marrying an ideal partner who does not exist in the world, they cannot guarantee that only good things will happen.  
If we think this way, we cannot help but discover that we are not capable of being self-sufficient in anything. There are many things we want to do, but we often find ourselves unable to do them.  
When we look at that, we realize that our lives are ours, and we think we are on our own path, but we know that we cannot do it as we please.

**Important Figures**  
This morning, let’s talk about the title 'Important Figures.' To become an outstanding figure, one must go through a training process. Everyone gathered here must want to become an important figure. When we say 'important figure,' it concludes that one must occupy a central position that surpasses the ordinary level. To do so, one must become a victorious standard in all environments and serve as a basis for comparison. To be a standard for comparison, one must distinguish between the complete and the incomplete. 

Then, what aspects must be superior to others for a human to become an important figure? We have five senses. In seeing, one must be superior to ordinary people. The same goes for hearing. In speaking, it must also be the same. In touching and feeling, one must excel in all aspects. Next is our heart. The heart itself must also be superior in its spending compared to ordinary people. Furthermore, in actions, one must stand out compared to others. 

That is a fact, but how can one achieve that? To see, hear, speak, and act better than others, one cannot just look, listen, speak, or act without training. One must have the content to surpass in all areas. To achieve that, how should one proceed? In seeing, one cannot just look; one must train to see with substance. Even if you read a book to study, you cannot just look at it. You must practice seeing and go through a training process; otherwise, it is impossible. 

The same goes for listening. You cannot just listen to music once. To gain detailed understanding, time and training are necessary. Speaking is the same. To speak better and stand out, there must be a training process. It is absolutely necessary to refine and train according to the content. 

Our actions are the same. Just doing something unfamiliar is not enough. One must act from a place of trained results. This is also true for how we use our minds and think. All of this must go through a training process. That is why meditation or prayer is a method of training the mind. 

**Qualities and Methods to Become an Important Person**  
To reach the position of being an important person, one must go through training in all aspects to become proficient and stand in the right place. Without that, one cannot become an important person. It is not something an ordinary person can do. One must accomplish what ordinary people cannot. 

To do that, it does not just happen. One must face many problems and go through training and trials, and moreover, one must become someone who can act on all issues with confidence to be an important person. 

In our daily lives, what kind of training are we undergoing? We are training in seeing, hearing, speaking, and acting throughout our lives. Ultimately, our lives are merely a training process. 

Whether one can live a life that possesses content and reaches a position of purpose and unity depends on whether one can complete that training process. Whether one can stand out as a standard of comparison in front of the entire environment is determined by this. 

One must see what ordinary people cannot see, hear what ordinary people cannot hear, speak what ordinary people cannot say, think what ordinary people cannot think, and act in ways ordinary people cannot act. If one does that, they will undoubtedly become an important person and a great person. 

How many such people does an organization have? This determines whether that organization can be central in front of the whole. Or, depending on how many such people a country has, it determines whether that country can become a global central nation. 

So, looking at our organization, what kind of people should we create you to be? What kind of person do you want to become? It is a fact that you want to become important people, and the church itself is trying to make you important people. 

To do that, we must provide training in various fields. We must create confident individuals by passing through diverse training. We must train the eyes to see what others cannot see. We must train the ears to hear what others cannot hear. We must train the mouth to speak what others cannot say. We must train the mind to think what others cannot think. No matter how well one sees, hears, speaks, and thinks, if they become a loser in action, everything falls apart. Therefore, we must make these people capable of breaking through any field rather than retreating. 

On the day of retreat, no matter how much training one has done and how well they are equipped, they become a loser. One must overcome even the most difficult problems. They must advance and be able to digest and overcome those problems with their own strength and ability to be recognized as a central being responsible for that problem, based on the victorious standard they have surpassed in that environment. 

**Where Important People, Families, Nations, and States Are Determined**  
So, you are now learning new things, hearing new things, learning new words, and training in an environment where you can think new thoughts. The content we learn is complex. The thoughts we have are complex. Now, is complexity bad? Complexity that has substance and unity becomes a precious thing.
